He is an Independent Solutions Architect who helps companies to make better and cheaper applications using Serverless architectures, Container based applications, and Hybrid Cloud solutions. He has experience speaking and teaching at the biggest conferences in Brazil and Americas, working as voluntary Leader of NodeBR, Javascript S√£o Paulo and Nerdz√£o Communities.
